 According to Vesta, the desi fridge is made of smooth, brown and red clay and works almost like an electronic fridge
 haalanki, yah desi upkaran electronic frij kii tarah barf nahin jamaa saktaa
 The design of the home fridge is based on the same centuries-old traditional method, with the help of which the food items have been saved during the summer in India
 unhone bataaya ki ek khaane vaale mitti ke is frij main pani bharne ke liye chhed banaaya gaya he
 The water filled in the hole is evenly spread in the roundness of the fridge

 Since this fridge is made of clay, it has innumerable fine holes
 in chhedon se pani ris-ris kar frij kii sataha par aata rahata he
 This water absorbs the heat of the refrigerator water and converts it into steam
 jab yah bhaap frij kii sataha se udati he to apane saath is desi upkaran ke bheetar kii garmi bhi le jaati he
